          AND ("fetchedat" IS NULL OR "fetchedat" < NOW() + INTERVAL '-1800 SECONDS')
          ORDER BY "fetchedat" NULLS FIRST, "queue", "jobid"
          FOR UPDATE SKIP LOCKED
          LIMIT 1
        )
        RETURNING "id" AS "Id", "jobid" AS "JobId", "queue" AS "Queue", "fetchedat" AS "FetchedAt";
